Look man, there are two types of people.. Grinders and Creators. Slogo and Jelly are grinders, they've found a formula that works and have refined that throughout the years The "3 creator collab." is a proven method, which doesn't work the same way as a duo, which is why they needed a replacement once you were gone. From what you're saying, it sounds like you're a Creator.. You're a person that enjoys creating something new, then moving onto the next challenge. You're not content to ride the wave of a proven formula, but would rather forge a new path where others have yet to tread. This could have been a cause for your depression as you grew more and more discontent with grinding out the same projects and the illusion of success made you possibly feel as though you "should" be happy with how your career was going, money was great, views were plentiful, popularity was high.   There is nothing wrong with being a Grinder or a Creator, the world needs both and both need each other. Without Creators, Grinders wouldn't would struggle with innovation and without Grinders, Creators would never have their ideas reach a wide audience. You did the right thing in stepping away and spreading your wings and from the sounds of it, you're really happy in life. I wish the best for you and everything you strive to achieve mate <3

Depression is really a terrible experience...  I also got severe depression for almost 2 years...  So,  I also felt and experience the same thing...  I tried to write webnovels,  as writting is one of my favorite activity to do but it didn't work out...  Writing while being in depression is very hard,  although ideas and inspirations still came to mind, just a single thought that is related to the cause of my depression, got me depressed once again. Thinking around and around those ideas until, my mind gets tired and cause me to sleep... And as time passed by,  depression dulled my imagination and the creativity of my mind...  And then I started recovering. I really really had a hard time adjusting to my surroundings...  But as time passed by I started treasuring every moment I had in my life, especially moments with my family... Its like my view of life changed after I experienced depression... I realized how important it is to have someone, who is close to you, to talk with, especially when you felt that you can't take it anymore... I also became more open about my thoughts and emotions after that experience...   - Don't mind me,  just wanna share my experience and thoughts...  ğŸ˜…
